<t>CREATE TABLE PolicyHolder (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50),
    age INT,
    policy_type VARCHAR(20),
    policy_amount DECIMAL
);


CREATE TABLE InsuranceCompany (
    company_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    company_name VARCHAR(50),
    location VARCHAR(50),
    contact_number VARCHAR(15)
);


CREATE TABLE Policy (
    policy_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    holder_id UUID REFERENCES PolicyHolder(id),
    company_id UUID REFERENCES InsuranceCompany(company_id),
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    premium DECIMAL
);
</t><s>UPDATE PolicyHolder SET name = 'Alice' WHERE id = '12345678-1234-5678-1234-567812345678'</s>
